<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt"><SPAN lang=EN-NZ><FONT color=#000000 face=Calibri size=3>There are some similar rows that can probably be considered as groups.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo3"><FONT color=#000000><SPAN lang=EN-NZ style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>·</FONT><SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-NZ><FONT face=Calibri size=3>Dependants, History, Logs and Preview screens are effectively read-only screens and consequently, the user always has access to these screens regardless of asset status.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo3"><FONT color=#000000><SPAN lang=EN-NZ style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>·</FONT><SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-NZ><FONT face=Calibri size=3>Permissions, Metadata Schemas, Layouts and Workflow (With the exception of approving or rejecting, as noted below) screens require admin access to make changes, so the user with write permission only, never has access.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt"><SPAN lang=EN-NZ><FONT color=#000000 face=Calibri size=3>The following table indicates which screens on the admin interface a user with write permission to assets with workflow applied that is not the approval step in workflow.</FONT></SPAN></P>
